# customer-details-capture-identifier >> customer-identifier-capture (OpenBookingApprovalFlow >> Multiple)

**Booking Flow:** OpenBookingApprovalFlow

**Opportunity Type:** Multiple

**Feature:** Details Capture / Customer Details identifier capture (Implemented) 

**Test:**  Customer identifier is reflected back at C2 and B

Identifier from the Customer supplied by Broker should be reflected back by booking system.

### Running only this test

```bash
npm start -- --runInBand test/features/details-capture/customer-details-capture-identifier/implemented/customer-identifier-capture-test.js
```
